MariaDB [osmakers]>


select
	o.id,
	o.endereco,
	t.nome as tipo,
	b.nome as bairro,
	date_format(o.data,'%d/%m/%y') as data
from
	oss o
	inner join tipos_de_os t ON o.id_tipo=t.id
	inner join bairros b ON b.id=o.id_bairro
where
	data='2019-11-17'
order by t.nome;


select *
from
	equipes inner join oss_equipes;
